\doxysubsubsection{Detailed Description}
Represents basic profile information about market instrument. 

Please see \href{http://www.dxfeed.com/downloads/documentation/dxFeed_Instrument_Profile_Format.pdf}{\texttt{ Instrument Profile Format documentation}} for complete description.

\index{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}!getBaseCurrency@{getBaseCurrency}}

\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{getBaseCurrency()}{getBaseCurrency()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::get\+Base\+Currency (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const \&\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

\Hypertarget{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_ae2bf08ae2cfbbd48c21a3cb279d55076}\label{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_ae2bf08ae2cfbbd48c21a3cb279d55076} 
\index{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}!getCFI@{getCFI}}
\index{getCFI@{getCFI}!dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{getCFI()}{getCFI()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::get\+CFI (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const \&\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Returns Classification of Financial Instruments code. 

It is a mandatory field for OPTION instruments as it is the only way to distinguish Call/\+Put type, American/\+European exercise, Cash/\+Physical delivery. It shall use six-\/letter CFI code from ISO 10962 standard. It is allowed to use \textquotesingle{}X\textquotesingle{} extensively and to omit trailing letters (assumed to be \textquotesingle{}X\textquotesingle{}). See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_10962}{\texttt{ ISO 10962 on Wikipedia}}. Example\+: "{}\+ESNTPB"{}, "{}\+ESXXXX"{}, "{}\+ES"{} , "{}\+OPASPS"{}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
CFI code. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a7f56b57f62f05beb50aaa8b6eb8faf1b}\label{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a7f56b57f62f05beb50aaa8b6eb8faf1b} 
\index{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}!getCountry@{getCountry}}
\index{getCountry@{getCountry}!dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{getCountry()}{getCountry()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::get\+Country (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const \&\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Returns country of origin (incorporation) of corresponding company or parent entity. 

It shall use two-\/letter country code from ISO 3166-\/1 standard. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_3166-1}{\texttt{ ISO 3166-\/1 on Wikipedia}}. Example\+: "{}\+US"{}, "{}\+RU"{}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The country of origin (incorporation) of corresponding company or parent entity. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{getCurrency()}{getCurrency()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::get\+Currency (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const \&\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Returns currency of quotation, pricing and trading. 

It shall use three-\/letter currency code from ISO 4217 standard. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_4217}{\texttt{ ISO 4217 on Wikipedia}}. Example\+: "{}\+USD"{}, "{}\+RUB"{}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Currency of quotation, pricing and trading. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Returns Committee on Uniform Security Identification Procedures code. 

It shall use nine-\/letter code assigned by CUSIP Services Bureau. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CUSIP}{\texttt{ CUSIP on Wikipedia}}. Example\+: "{}38259\+P508"{}.

\Hypertarget{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a4f4fc65dcdcc2a2f14e4614ce13a5be5}\label{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a4f4fc65dcdcc2a2f14e4614ce13a5be5} 
\index{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}!getMMY@{getMMY}}
\index{getMMY@{getMMY}!dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{getMMY()}{getMMY()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::get\+MMY (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const \&\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Returns maturity month-\/year as provided for corresponding FIX tag (200). 

It can use several different formats depending on data source\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item YYYYMM  if only year and month are specified 
\item YYYYMMDD  if full date is specified 
\item YYYYMMwN  if week number (within a month) is specified 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The maturity month-\/year as provided for corresponding FIX tag (200). 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a12c01c85ec013cb6a98d16de1589059d}\label{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a12c01c85ec013cb6a98d16de1589059d} 
\index{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}!getOPOL@{getOPOL}}
\index{getOPOL@{getOPOL}!dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{getOPOL()}{getOPOL()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::get\+OPOL (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const \&\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Returns official Place Of Listing, the organization that have listed this instrument. 

Instruments with multiple listings shall use separate profiles for each listing. It shall use Market Identifier Code (MIC) from ISO 10383 standard. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_10383}{\texttt{ ISO 10383 on Wikipedia}} or \href{http://www.iso15022.org/MIC/homepageMIC.htm}{\texttt{ MIC homepage}}. Example\+: "{}\+XNAS"{}, "{}\+RTSX"{}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The official Place Of Listing, the organization that have listed this instrument. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_adc59b887cb7047c64ab9419b6c18330c}\label{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_adc59b887cb7047c64ab9419b6c18330c} 
\index{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}!getOptionType@{getOptionType}}
\index{getOptionType@{getOptionType}!dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{getOptionType()}{getOptionType()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::get\+Option\+Type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const \&\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Returns type of option. 

It shall use one of following values\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item STAN = Standard Options 
\item LEAP = Long-\/term Equity Antici\+Pation Securities 
\item SDO = Special Dated Options 
\item BINY = Binary Options 
\item FLEX = FLexible EXchange Options 
\item VSO = Variable Start Options 
\item RNGE = Range 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The type of option. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_ad8b2cefdf4a7b2c90fac7a9a797ff943}\label{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_ad8b2cefdf4a7b2c90fac7a9a797ff943} 
\index{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}!setCFI@{setCFI}}
\index{setCFI@{setCFI}!dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{setCFI()}{setCFI()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{void}} dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::set\+CFI (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{cfi }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Changes Classification of Financial Instruments code. 

It is a mandatory field for OPTION instruments as it is the only way to distinguish Call/\+Put type, American/\+European exercise, Cash/\+Physical delivery. It shall use six-\/letter CFI code from ISO 10962 standard. It is allowed to use \textquotesingle{}X\textquotesingle{} extensively and to omit trailing letters (assumed to be \textquotesingle{}X\textquotesingle{}). See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_10962}{\texttt{ ISO 10962 on Wikipedia}}. Example\+: "{}\+ESNTPB"{}, "{}\+ESXXXX"{}, "{}\+ES"{} , "{}\+OPASPS"{}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cfi} & CFI code. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

It shall use two-\/letter country code from ISO 3166-\/1 standard. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_3166-1}{\texttt{ ISO 3166-\/1 on Wikipedia}}. Example\+: "{}\+US"{}, "{}\+RU"{}.

Changes maturity month-\/year as provided for corresponding FIX tag (200). 

It can use several different formats depending on data source\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item YYYYMM  if only year and month are specified 
\item YYYYMMDD  if full date is specified 
\item YYYYMMwN  if week number (within a month) is specified 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyParams}

Changes official Place Of Listing, the organization that have listed this instrument. 

Instruments with multiple listings shall use separate profiles for each listing. It shall use Market Identifier Code (MIC) from ISO 10383 standard. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_10383}{\texttt{ ISO 10383 on Wikipedia}} or \href{http://www.iso15022.org/MIC/homepageMIC.htm}{\texttt{ MIC homepage}}. Example\+: "{}\+XNAS"{}, "{}\+RTSX"{}

Changes type of option. 

It shall use one of following values\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item STAN = Standard Options 
\item LEAP = Long-\/term Equity Antici\+Pation Securities 
\item SDO = Special Dated Options 
\item BINY = Binary Options 
\item FLEX = FLexible EXchange Options 
\item VSO = Variable Start Options 
\item RNGE = Range 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{setSIC()}{setSIC()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{void}} dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::set\+SIC (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::int32\+\_\+t}]{sic }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Changes Standard Industrial Classification. 

It shall use four-\/digit number from SIC catalog. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Industrial_Classification}{\texttt{ SIC on Wikipedia}} or \href{https://www.osha.gov/pls/imis/sic_manual.html}{\texttt{ SIC structure}}. Example\+: "{}7371"{}.

\Hypertarget{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a2a103848f2bc6dbe2e15d859171cd3a7}\label{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a2a103848f2bc6dbe2e15d859171cd3a7} 
\index{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}!withCFI@{withCFI}}
\index{withCFI@{withCFI}!dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{withCFI()}{withCFI()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile}{Instrument\+Profile}} \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::with\+CFI (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{cfi }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Changes Classification of Financial Instruments code. 

It is a mandatory field for OPTION instruments as it is the only way to distinguish Call/\+Put type, American/\+European exercise, Cash/\+Physical delivery. It shall use six-\/letter CFI code from ISO 10962 standard. It is allowed to use \textquotesingle{}X\textquotesingle{} extensively and to omit trailing letters (assumed to be \textquotesingle{}X\textquotesingle{}). See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_10962}{\texttt{ ISO 10962 on Wikipedia}}. Example\+: "{}\+ESNTPB"{}, "{}\+ESXXXX"{}, "{}\+ES"{} , "{}\+OPASPS"{}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cfi} & CFI code. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The current instrument profile. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a26f166e35c4aede0a08c56579a1554ea}\label{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a26f166e35c4aede0a08c56579a1554ea} 
\index{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}!withCFIShared@{withCFIShared}}
\index{withCFIShared@{withCFIShared}!dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{withCFIShared()}{withCFIShared()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a473c8c382c869283bd1758524250412e}{Instrument\+Profile\+::\+Ptr}} dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::with\+CFIShared (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{cfi }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Changes Classification of Financial Instruments code. 

It is a mandatory field for OPTION instruments as it is the only way to distinguish Call/\+Put type, American/\+European exercise, Cash/\+Physical delivery. It shall use six-\/letter CFI code from ISO 10962 standard. It is allowed to use \textquotesingle{}X\textquotesingle{} extensively and to omit trailing letters (assumed to be \textquotesingle{}X\textquotesingle{}). See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_10962}{\texttt{ ISO 10962 on Wikipedia}}. Example\+: "{}\+ESNTPB"{}, "{}\+ESXXXX"{}, "{}\+ES"{} , "{}\+OPASPS"{}.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Please do not use this method unless the object was created with {\ttfamily std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile}{Instrument\+Profile}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}(new Instrument\+Profile(...))} or {\ttfamily std\+::make\+\_\+shared\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile}{Instrument\+Profile}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}(...)}
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cfi} & CFI code. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile}{Instrument\+Profile}} \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::with\+Country (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{country }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Changes country of origin (incorporation) of corresponding company or parent entity. 

It shall use two-\/letter country code from ISO 3166-\/1 standard. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_3166-1}{\texttt{ ISO 3166-\/1 on Wikipedia}}. Example\+: "{}\+US"{}, "{}\+RU"{}.

Changes Industry Classification Benchmark. 

It shall use four-\/digit number from ICB catalog. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Industry_Classification_Benchmark}{\texttt{ ICB on Wikipedia}} or \href{http://www.icbenchmark.com/}{\texttt{ ICB homepage}}. Example\+: "{}9535"{}.

\end{DoxyParams}

The current instrument profile.

Changes International Securities Identifying Number. 

It shall use twelve-\/letter code from ISO 6166 standard. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_6166}{\texttt{ ISO 6166 on Wikipedia}} or \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Securities_Identifying_Number}{\texttt{ ISIN on Wikipedia}}. Example\+: "{}\+DE0007100000"{}, "{}\+US38259\+P5089"{}.

\Hypertarget{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_aeda8d441143c622ff9c66f9a2f97ba60}\label{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_aeda8d441143c622ff9c66f9a2f97ba60} 
\index{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}!withMMY@{withMMY}}
\index{withMMY@{withMMY}!dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{withMMY()}{withMMY()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile}{Instrument\+Profile}} \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::with\+MMY (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{mmy }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Changes maturity month-\/year as provided for corresponding FIX tag (200). 

It can use several different formats depending on data source\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item YYYYMM  if only year and month are specified 
\item YYYYMMDD  if full date is specified 
\item YYYYMMwN  if week number (within a month) is specified 
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mmy} & The maturity month-\/year as provided for corresponding FIX tag (200). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The current instrument profile. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a1945892ea76783a93e31fdffb467f9db}\label{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a1945892ea76783a93e31fdffb467f9db}

Changes maturity month-\/year as provided for corresponding FIX tag (200). 

It can use several different formats depending on data source\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item YYYYMM  if only year and month are specified 
\item YYYYMMDD  if full date is specified 
\item YYYYMMwN  if week number (within a month) is specified 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\Hypertarget{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a99706699d96bee370964dc0604ed1850}\label{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile_a99706699d96bee370964dc0604ed1850} 
\index{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}!withOPOL@{withOPOL}}
\index{withOPOL@{withOPOL}!dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile@{dxfcpp::InstrumentProfile}}
\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{withOPOL()}{withOPOL()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile}{Instrument\+Profile}} \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::with\+OPOL (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{opol }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Changes official Place Of Listing, the organization that have listed this instrument. 

Instruments with multiple listings shall use separate profiles for each listing. It shall use Market Identifier Code (MIC) from ISO 10383 standard. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_10383}{\texttt{ ISO 10383 on Wikipedia}} or \href{http://www.iso15022.org/MIC/homepageMIC.htm}{\texttt{ MIC homepage}}. Example\+: "{}\+XNAS"{}, "{}\+RTSX"{}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em opol} & The official Place Of Listing, the organization that have listed this instrument. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The current instrument profile. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{withOptionType()}{withOptionType()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile}{Instrument\+Profile}} \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::with\+Option\+Type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structdxfcpp_1_1_shared_entity_aa117214d0b4e4fc6979400eff315a8d3}{const}} std\+::string \&}]{option\+Type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Changes type of option. 

It shall use one of following values\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item STAN = Standard Options 
\item LEAP = Long-\/term Equity Antici\+Pation Securities 
\item SDO = Special Dated Options 
\item BINY = Binary Options 
\item FLEX = FLexible EXchange Options 
\item VSO = Variable Start Options 
\item RNGE = Range 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

The current instrument profile.

Changes Stock Exchange Daily Official List. 

It shall use seven-\/letter code assigned by London Stock Exchange. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SEDOL}{\texttt{ SEDOL on Wikipedia}} or \href{http://www.londonstockexchange.com/en-gb/products/informationproducts/sedol/}{\texttt{ SEDOL on LSE}}. Example\+: "{}2310967"{}, "{}5766857"{}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classdxfcpp_1_1_instrument_profile}{Instrument\+Profile}} \& dxfcpp\+::\+Instrument\+Profile\+::with\+SIC (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::int32\+\_\+t}]{sic }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Changes Standard Industrial Classification. 

It shall use four-\/digit number from SIC catalog. See \href{http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Industrial_Classification}{\texttt{ SIC on Wikipedia}} or \href{https://www.osha.gov/pls/imis/sic_manual.html}{\texttt{ SIC structure}}. Example\+: "{}7371"{}.
